'ROOSEVELT, WILLKIE, TIED FOR EC, ELECTION WILL GO TO HOUSE; Marvel beats Truman, Townshend holds off Tunnel, Reps Gain in House, but Dems hold Majorities'

Neither you nor President Roosevelt have won a majority in the electoral college. It’s unclear what will happen now. Democrats hold a narrow majority of congressional delegations, but even a handful of defections can put Willkie in the White House, and isolationist sentiment still holds strong throughout most of the nation.
